   NOTES:  I got to the end of chapter 10 before I stopped.  
There are some places along the way where I did not 
insert the variant (because they were in Latin, too 
complicated/ambiguous for me, or both).  Those places 
are boxed on the hard copy.  Let me know if I can help 
sort anything out.               (Pax,)  Max.
   NOTES 2 (Allen K.): I did 11:1 through 14:5.  Where a 
superscripted minus sign is used in the apparatus, I 
have typed the minus sign inside the superscript markers 
rather than outside them; e.g., I type <Lt>L'</><s-19>s 
instead of <Lt>L'</>-<s19>s. The placement inside 
corresponds much more closely to the visual impact of 
the hard copy than does the placement outside and, more 
important, it corresponds more closely conceptually.  It 
also distinguishes this use of the keyboarded hyphen 
from the keyboarded hyphen used to signify a group such 
as 46-52, where the hyphen is not superscripted.  Dr. 
Bob agrees that the inside placement is preferable over 
the outside placement which is written in the original 
guide.  Previous work using the older outside placement 
is thus inconsistent with this newer style and will have 
to be corrected in the end.  I apologize for the 
inevitable mistakes and errors of method that escaped 
me.
